hourlyActs <- read.csv('hourlyActs.csv')
dailyActs <- read.csv('dailyActs.csv')
minActsN <- read.csv('minActsN.csv')
minSleep <- read.csv('minSleep.csv')
sleepDay <- read.csv('sleepDay.csv')
weightLog <- read.csv('weightLog.csv')
hrate_sec <- read.csv('hrate_sec.csv')
# change to date type
dailyActs$ DailyActsDate <- as.Date(dailyActs$DailyActsDate, '%m/%d/%Y')
hourlyActs$HourlyDate <- as.Date(hourlyActs$ActivityHour, '%m/%d/%Y')
minActsN$MinuteDates <- as.Date(minActsN$DateMinute, '%m/%d/%Y')
minSleep$MinSleepDate <- as.Date(minSleep$MinSleepDateTime, '%m/%d/%Y')
sleepDay$SleepDate <- as.Date(sleepDay$SleepDateTime, '%m/%d/%Y')
weightLog$WeightDate <- as.Date(weightLog$WeightDateTime, '%m/%d/%Y')
hrate_sec$HRateDate <- as.Date(hrate_sec$HRateDateTime, '%m/%d/%Y')
# change to time type
dailyActs$DailyActsDate <- chron(times.=(format(strptime(dailyActs$DailyActsDate, '%m/%d/%Y %r'), '%H:%M:%S')))
hourlyActs$Hour <- chron(times.=(format(strptime(hourlyActs$ActivityHour, '%m/%d/%Y %r'), '%H:%M:%S')))
minActsN$Minutes <- chron(times.=(format(strptime(minActsN$DateMinute, '%m/%d/%Y %r'), '%H:%M:%S')))
minSleep$SleepMinutes <- chron(times.=(format(strptime(minSleep$MinSleepDateTime, '%m/%d/%Y %r'), '%H:%M:%S')))
sleepDay$SleepTime <- chron(times.=(format(strptime(sleepDay$SleepDateTime, '%m/%d/%Y %r'), '%H:%M:%S')))
weightLog$WeightTime <- chron(times.=(format(strptime(weightLog$WeightDateTime, '%m/%d/%Y %r'), '%H:%M:%S')))
hrate_sec$HRateTime <- chron(times.=(format(strptime(hrate_sec$HRateDateTime, '%m/%d/%Y %r'), '%H:%M:%S')))

# distinct count of report per user
mod_smart %>%
group_by(IsManualReport)%>%
summarise(WeightUserCount=length(unique(Id))) %>%
arrange(desc(WeightUserCount)) %>%
drop_na()
# distinct count of Feature use per users(Id)
mod_smart %>%
group_by(SmartFeatures)%>%
summarise(UserCount=length(unique(Id))) %>%
arrange(desc(UserCount))
# top 10 most used features by hour
mod_smart %>%
mutate(hour_of_day=hours(Time)) %>%
group_by(hour_of_day, SmartFeatures) %>%
summarise(Total=n()) %>%
arrange(hour_of_day, desc(Total)) %>%
drop_na(hour_of_day) %>% # drops na values in from hour after conversion
slice(1:10)

#stacked area chart---minutes
mm <- mod_mins %>%
mutate(Minutes=minutes(Time)) %>%
group_by(Minutes, Features) %>%
summarise(Total_Count= n()) %>%
ggplot(aes(x=Minutes, y=Total_Count, fill=Features)) +
geom_area(color="white") +
ggtitle('Minute Frequency of Minute-Wide Features') +
scale_y_continuous(labels = scales::comma) +
ylab("Frequency") +
theme(plot.title = element_text(size=10, face="bold", ),
axis.title.x=element_blank(),
axis.title.y=element_blank(),
legend.text = element_text(size=8),
legend.title = element_blank())
am <- mod_mins %>%
mutate(Minutes=minutes(Time)) %>%
group_by(Minutes, Features) %>%
summarise(Average= mean(Value)) %>%
ggplot(aes(x=Minutes, y=Average, fill=Features)) +
geom_area(color="white") +
ggtitle('Minute Averages of Minute-Wide Features') +
scale_y_continuous(labels = scales::comma) +
ylab("Average") +
theme(plot.title = element_text(size=10, face="bold", ),
axis.title.x=element_blank(),
axis.title.y=element_blank(),
legend.text = element_text(size=8),
legend.title = element_blank())
plot_grid(mm, am, nrow=2, align="v")
mod_mins$Features <- factor(mod_mins$Features, levels=c("Steps", "Calories", "Intensity"))
wm <- mod_mins %>%
mutate(Weekday=wday(Date, label=TRUE)) %>%
group_by(Weekday, Features) %>%
summarise(Count = n()) %>%
arrange(Weekday) %>%
ggplot(aes(x=Weekday, y=Count, fill=Features)) +
geom_col() +
ggtitle('Weekday Frequency of Minute-Wide Features') +
scale_y_continuous(labels = scales::comma) +
theme(legend.position = "none",
plot.title = element_text(face="bold", size=10),
axis.title.x=element_blank(),
axis.title.y=element_blank()) +
facet_grid(vars(Features))
wam <- mod_mins %>%
mutate(Weekday=wday(Date, label=TRUE)) %>%
group_by(Weekday, Features) %>%
summarise(Average = mean(Value)) %>%
arrange(Weekday) %>%
ggplot(aes(x=Weekday, y=Average, fill=Features)) +
geom_bar(stat="identity", position = "dodge") +
ggtitle('Weekday Average of Minute-Wide Features') +
scale_y_continuous(labels = scales::comma) +
theme(plot.title = element_text(face="bold", size=10),

mod_sm %>%
group_by(Category) %>%
summarise(Total=n()) %>%
mutate(percentage=round(Total*100/sum(Total), 3)) %>%
arrange(desc(Category)) %>%
mutate(y_pos = cumsum(percentage)-0.5*percentage) %>%
ggplot(aes(x=2, y=percentage, fill=Category))+
geom_bar(stat="identity", color="white") +
ggtitle('Total Smart Feature Category Use') +
coord_polar(theta = "y", start=0)+
geom_text(aes(y=y_pos, label=paste0(Category, sep="\n", percentage, "%")), color="black", size=6)+
theme_void() +
xlim(0.6,2.6)

coord_polar(theta = "y", start=0)+
geom_text(aes(y=y_pos, label=paste0(Category, sep="\n", percentage, "%")), color="black", size=3)+
theme(legend.position = "none") +
theme_void() +
xlim(0.6,2.6)

##dailyActs vs dailySteps

#dailyActs vs dailyInts

#join dailyActs & sleepDay datsets by Id & date as keys
daily <- full_join(dailyActs, sleepDay, by=join_by(DailyId==SleepDayId, DailyActsDate==SleepDate), keep=TRUE) # keep=TRUE keeps matching column
gc()
# join daily data and hourly dataset
## merge smaller dataset to larger data set to keep order in Id, Date and Time
daily_hour <- full_join(daily, hourlyActs, by=join_by(DailyId==HourlyId, DailyActsDate==HourlyDate, SleepTime==Hour), keep=TRUE)
# clear previous joined files
rm(daily, hourlyActs, dailyActs, sleepDay)
gc()
# join minute datasets together
minutes <- full_join(minActs, minSleep, by=join_by(MinActsId==MinSleepId, MinuteDate==MinSleepDate, Minutes==SleepMinutes), keep=TRUE)
rm(minActs, minSleep)
gc()
# combine daily_hour &  minutes; use hour as next longest available time format
d_hr_min <- full_join(daily_hour, minutes, by=join_by(DailyId==MinActsId, DailyActsDate==MinuteDate, Hour==Minutes), keep=TRUE)
gc()
rm(daily_hour, minutes)
gc()
# join d_hr_min + hrate_sec
smarties <- full_join(d_hr_min, hrate_sec, by=join_by(DailyId==HRateId, DailyActsDate==HRateDate, Minutes==HRateTime), keep=TRUE)
gc()
# join smarties + weight Log
smart <- full_join(smarties, weightLog, by=join_by(DailyId==WeightId, DailyActsDate==WeightDate, HRateTime==WeightTime), keep=TRUE)
#clear environment
rm(smarties, d_hr_min, hrate_sec, weightLog)
gc()
# set directory
setwd('C:/Users/Leopoldine/Desktop/Mine/Coding Projects & Portfolio/Bellabeat/01_tidy_data')
#export file
write.csv(smart, 'smart.csv', row.names = FALSE)

smartDev$DailyId <- ifelse(is.na(smartDev$DailyId), smartDev$MinSleepId, smartDev$DailyId)
